SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]

SELECT TOP(2) [x].[Name], [x].[Owner], [x].[Amount], [x].[CreationDate], [x].[BudgetId], [x].[UserId], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT CASE
            WHEN EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM [Expenses] AS [e]
                WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [e].[UserBudgetBudgetId])
            THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
        END
    ) = 1
    THEN [x].[Amount] - (
        SELECT SUM([y].[Amount])
        FROM [Expenses] AS [y]
        WHERE [x].[BudgetId] = [y].[UserBudgetBudgetId]
    ) ELSE 0E0
END AS [Balance]
FROM [Budgets] AS [x]
WHERE ([x].[BudgetId] = @__id_0) AND ([x].[IsDeleted] = 0)
ORDER BY [x].[BudgetId]
